1546777452871 UID: 315235620400136204 CID: 531447079902642187 U: huehuehue Msg: **BIG USELESS LIST OF VIVENTEM DRONES** that is reposted from pinned messages in <#523960038939951104> 

*BIPED* - A thin, multirole 9ft tall chassis made out of a strong, glinting metal, comes with 2 arms but can have up to 6 arms attached afterwards. Usually carries an assault rifle or sniper rifle. Usually sent out for defense/zerg rushing/guarding important targets, but can be reconfigured to serve different roles.
*SOLDIER* - Bulkier, tougher version of the Biped, allowed all sorts of heavy duty weapons like LMGs and handheld miniguns, also not equipped with the first law that most Viventem drones have. Meant for offense/heavy defense/guarding very important targets such as presidents or resources.
*TRIPED* - Small drone with 3 legs that skitters across buildings/ships, making repairs or augmenting systems/weapons/whatever.
*CONSTRUCTOR* - Flying version of the triped.
*AUGMENTER* - Small flying drones that offer superior mechanical prosthetics to humans to replace normal limbs. Said limbs usually have an extra function or two.
*HEAVY LIFTER* -Large, bulky triped drone that is usually sent for mining operations. Can carry anything that fits in the top, from glowing suspendium to commodities to bodies/body parts.
*SPEAKER/SCREEN* - Portable flying public service announcements.
*POD* - "Representatives" of the viventem, usually sent out with the intention of "help stuff", very unpredictable, may go rogue and begin forceful conversion of an area.
*QUADRUPED* - Massive walking fortress dotted with guns of varying sizes, and crewed by a healthy amount of bipeds and tripeds.
*SPIDER* - A massive brass spider drone that disperses triped drones and constructors when needed.
*CARRIER* - A flying airbase that dispenses various flying drones.
*TRANSPORT* - What it says on the tin, can change size to a maximum of 500 meters to accommodate cargo. Evt: [object Object]
